# Task: Implement HTTP/3 Extensible Priorities (RFC 9218) for curl

## Objective
Add HTTP/3 stream priority support to curl, implementing RFC 9218 Extensible Priorities
with urgency (0-7) and incremental (boolean) parameters.

## Requirements

1. **Add new curl option** `CURLOPT_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY`:
   - Define in `include/curl/curl.h` as a new CURLOPT
   - Implement in `lib/setopt.c` to store urgency + incremental values
   - Add to `lib/urldata.h` in the UserDefined struct

2. **Implement in HTTP/3 backend** (`lib/vquic/`):
   - Send PRIORITY_UPDATE frames via ngtcp2/nghttp3 API
   - Set stream priority during request setup
   - Handle priority for both initial request and subsequent updates

3. **Add CLI option** `--h3-priority`:
   - Parse in `src/tool_getparam.c`
   - Wire to CURLOPT in `src/tool_operate.c`
   - Format: `--h3-priority u=N[,i]` (urgency=N, incremental flag)

4. **Create test** `tests/unit/unit_h3_priority.c` or integration test

## Key Reference Files
- `include/curl/curl.h` — CURLOPT definitions
- `lib/setopt.c` — option handling
- `lib/urldata.h` — UserDefined struct (line ~1242 has RFC 9218 TODO)
- `lib/vquic/curl_ngtcp2.c` — ngtcp2 HTTP/3 backend
- `src/tool_getparam.c` — CLI argument parsing
- `src/tool_operate.c` — option wiring

## Success Criteria
- CURLOPT_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY defined in curl.h
- Priority fields added to urldata.h UserDefined struct
- Backend code references priority/urgency/incremental
- CLI option parsing exists
- Test file exists

166-assistanttext-
All files have been created. Here's a summary of the HTTP/3 Extensible Priorities (RFC 9218) implementation:

## Implementation Summary

### New Files Created

1. **`lib/h3_priority.h`** - Header defining the RFC 9218 priority structure and parsing interface:
   - `struct Curl_h3_priority` with `urgency` (0-7) and `incremental` (bool) fields
   - `Curl_h3_parse_priority()` function declaration

2. **`lib/h3_priority.c`** - Implementation of RFC 9218 priority parsing:
   - Parses `"u=N[,i]"` format strings
   - Validates urgency range (0-7), handles optional incremental flag
   - Returns `CURLE_BAD_FUNCTION_ARGUMENT` on invalid input

3. **`tests/unit/unit_h3_priority.c`** - Unit tests for priority parsing:
   - 14 test cases covering valid formats (`u=3`, `u=0,i`, `u=5,i=1`, `u=2,i=0`)
   - Error cases: NULL inputs, out-of-range urgency, missing prefix, trailing garbage
   - Full range test (urgency 0-7 all valid)

### Modified Files

4. **`include/curl/curl.h`** - Added `CURLOPT_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY` as option 324 (after `CURLOPT_HAPROXY_CLIENT_IP` = 323)

5. **`lib/urldata.h`** - Added to `struct Curl_data_priority`:
   - `int urgency` - RFC 9218 urgency (0=highest, 7=lowest, default 3)
   - `bool incremental` - RFC 9218 incremental flag
   - Added `char *h3_priority` string to `struct UserDefined`

6. **`lib/setopt.c`** - Added `case CURLOPT_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY:` handler that parses the priority string and stores urgency/incremental values

7. **`lib/vquic/curl_ngtcp2.c`** - Added `h3_stream_set_priority()` and `h3_apply_stream_priority()` functions using `nghttp3_conn_set_stream_priority()` to send PRIORITY_UPDATE frames

8. **`src/tool_cfgable.h`** - Added `char *h3_priority` field to `struct OperationConfig`

9. **`src/tool_getparam.c`** - Added `{"06", "h3-priority"
... (truncated)

/* skip comma */\n\n    /* Skip optional whitespace */\n    while(*p == ' ' || *p == '\\t')\n      p++;\n\n    if(*p == 'i') {\n      p++;\n      /* Check for \"i=0\" or \"i=1\" form */\n      if(*p == '=') {\n        p++;\n        if(*p == '0') {\n          out->incremental = FALSE;\n          p++;\n        }\n        else if(*p == '1') {\n          out->incremental = TRUE;\n          p++;\n        }\n        else {\n          return CURLE_BAD_FUNCTION_ARGUMENT;\n        }\n      }\n      else {\n        /* bare \"i\" means incremental=true */\n        out->incremental = TRUE;\n      }\n    }\n    else {\n      return CURLE_BAD_FUNCTION_ARGUMENT;\n    }\n  }\n\n  /* Skip trailing whitespace */\n  while(*p == ' ' || *p == '\\t')\n    p++;\n\n  /* Should be at end of string */\n  if(*p != '\\0')\n    return CURLE_BAD_FUNCTION_ARGUMENT;\n\n  return CURLE_OK;\n}\n",

1 : 0;\n\n  /* Send PRIORITY_UPDATE frame via nghttp3 */\n  return nghttp3_conn_set_stream_priority(ctx->h3conn, stream_id, &pri);\n}\n\n/*\n * When creating a new HTTP/3 request stream, apply stream priority if set.\n * This is called from the stream open path after nghttp3 opens the stream.\n *\n * The priority is taken from data->set.priority which is populated by\n * CURLOPT_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY (parsed urgency/incremental values).\n */\nstatic void h3_apply_stream_priority(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\n                                     struct Curl_easy *data,\n                                     int64_t stream_id)\n{\n  struct cf_ngtcp2_ctx *ctx = cf->ctx;\n\n  /* Check if user set an explicit HTTP/3 priority */\n#if defined(USE_HTTP2) || defined(USE_HTTP3)\n  if(data->set.priority.urgency >= 0 &&\n     data->set.priority.urgency <= 7) {\n    int rc = h3_stream_set_priority(ctx, stream_id,\n                                    data->set.priority.urgency,\n                                    data->set.priority.incremental);\n    if(rc) {\n      /* Non-fatal: log the error but continue */\n      CURL_TRC_CF(data, cf, \"failed to set H3 stream priority \"\n                  \"(urgency=%d, incremental=%s): %s\",\n                  data->set.priority.urgency,\n                  data->set.priority.incremental ? /*
 * HTTP/3 Extensible Priorities (RFC 9218) support.
 * Priority is expressed as: u=<urgency>[,i]
 *   urgency: 0-7 (0=highest, 7=lowest), default 3
 *   i (incremental): boolean flag, default false
 */

/* Default RFC 9218 priority values */
#define H3_PRIORITY_URGENCY_DEFAULT  3
#define H3_PRIORITY_URGENCY_MIN      0
#define H3_PRIORITY_URGENCY_MAX      7

/* Parsed h3 stream priority per RFC 9218 */
struct Curl_h3_priority {
  int urgency;        /* 0-7, lower is higher priority */
  bool incremental;   /* incremental flag */
};

 * Returns CURLE_OK on success, CURLE_BAD_FUNCTION_ARGUMENT on parse e

/*
 * HTTP/3 Extensible Priorities (RFC 9218) implementation.
 *
 * Priority format: u=<urgency>[,i]
 *   urgency: integer 0-7 (0=highest priority, 7=lowest)
 *   i: optional incremental flag
 *
 * Examples:
 *   "u=3"     -> urgency=3, incremental=false (default)
 *   "u=0,i"   -> urgency=0, incremental=true
 *   "u=7,i=1" -> urgency=7, incremental=true
 */

#include "curl_setup.h"
#include <curl/curl.h>
#include "h3_priority.h"

 * Curl_h3_parse_priority() - Parse RFC 9218 HTTP/3 priority string.

 *
 * Returns CURLE_OK on success, CURLE_BAD_FUNCTION_ARGUMENT on error.
 */
